    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

  <span id="freeText13139395432730446635" style="display:none"><i>"Why didn’t you kill me like I asked?" <br />"I didn’t feel like it." </i> <br /> <br />Twenty-two year old Shoshanna has suffered depression since she was a child. <br /> <br />Once, she actually tried to end it all, but failed miserably. Since then, she has been struggling to keep a promise she made to her parents... one that she has regretted making ever since. <br /> <br />One day though, she sees news about a killer on the loose, who appears to be targeting girls around her age. Then an idea pops in her head: <i>What if I could end it all? Why does an innocent girl have to lose her life when she doesn’t want to? When I am stuck here living a life that I don’t want to live. </i> <br /> <br />So she decides to go on the hunt, find the predator, and… offer herself as a willing prey. <br /> <br />But is she going to get what she wants, or is she going to get more than she bargained for?</span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2672465416" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16866172517069214346">This book took me completely by surprise - by reading the blurb I was expecting a different story. A serial killer in the city and a young woman who wants to die. However, I was not expecting it to take a turn for the paranormal and the serial killer to be a vampire.<br/><br/>I had some problems with Shoshanna's determination to die at first but the more I read about her life, the more I could see her point. She went through so much and never told anybody about it, not even her parents. And why did they n</span>
  <span id="freeText16866172517069214346" style="display:none">This book took me completely by surprise - by reading the blurb I was expecting a different story. A serial killer in the city and a young woman who wants to die. However, I was not expecting it to take a turn for the paranormal and the serial killer to be a vampire.<br /><br />I had some problems with Shoshanna's determination to die at first but the more I read about her life, the more I could see her point. She went through so much and never told anybody about it, not even her parents. And why did they never question where her anxiety of being touched come from?! She said it herself: She went into this hospital with a depression and came out with more trauma.<br /><br />I have read a lot of vampire books - both good ones and some not so good and even some bad ones. This one here was surprisingly good and got better with each chapter. In the end, I hardly couldn't put it down and when I was finished, I wished for more. Tobias was an interesting character and the idea with the rare blood born vampires who need a balance was intriguing. I hope Amber is writing more about this interesting couple, I very much enjoyed reading this story and seeing Shoshanna slowly opening up to Tobias, I would love to see how this turns out.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16866172517069214346" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2251262278" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2251262278" />
    <a title="Alaina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/76272621-alaina"><img alt="Alaina" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2251262278?book_show_action=true">Jan 09, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alaina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alaina" href="/user/show/76272621-alaina">Alaina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781680304220" href="/book/show/26397073-the-sweetest-kill">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2251262278" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14330362803930160326"> The sweetest kill is filled with twists and turns that will never let you think of putting it down. Shoshanna has been on the edge of her sanity her whole life, from her complicated family to her mysterious and dark past. She has always struggled and thinks the only way out is to end it, leaving you with more questions than answers. This story is breathtaking and will let you experience every single one of her emotions. Her journey is frustrating and inspiring. You will find yourself relating t</span>
  <span id="freeText14330362803930160326" style="display:none"> The sweetest kill is filled with twists and turns that will never let you think of putting it down. Shoshanna has been on the edge of her sanity her whole life, from her complicated family to her mysterious and dark past. She has always struggled and thinks the only way out is to end it, leaving you with more questions than answers. This story is breathtaking and will let you experience every single one of her emotions. Her journey is frustrating and inspiring. You will find yourself relating to her issues and understanding her motives for her actions. Anne Lee is one of my favorite authors. When I hear her voice through the pages I feel transported into the book. I never at any time feel lost or uninterested. Her take on vampires and their lifestyles is intriguing, I find myself reading a lot of vampire novels and this one surprised me with its unique spin. This murder is definitely not what you expect, I imagine him to be a sight for sore eyes; and I am guessing that Shoshanna thinks so to. There is a fun mixture of genres including romance, fantasy and drama. Another thing I value about this author is that you can find her on Wattpad, which is a free app that you can download on Android or Apple. This is where I found her and was first trapped by her words. This is a must read for anyone who wants to a good unique read.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14330362803930160326" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('e/BaTGLshbVySAwDNQ3tOK4eikh8ikIpPdx+ahoSJW0ThRHC1nH9B1H3XMF1gDegUtXRFCW3LlsyunjN7cQIPA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('p9NS4Vy13g8Irc5itMWzdwkwCUQIvFfMDx5/gxnFKynPphlv6CimvSsSnqD0SGnv9ftSGFGBO74AeHkk7hMGeA==')})
  }

In mere days Amy will be condemned to a stifling, loveless marriage, and she sees no way out—until the devastating fire of 1666 sweeps through London, and tragedy lands her in the arms of a dashing nobleman who knows a diamond in the rough when he sees it…Colin Chase, the Earl of Greystone, has his future all figured out. He’s restoring his crumbling castle and estate to its former glory, and the key to its completion is his rich bride-to-be. But the Great Fire lays waste to his plans, saddling him with trouble—in the form of a lowly shopkeeper’s daughter with whom he’s most inconveniently falling in love...<\/span>\n  <a
